<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:настроить.html>настро́ивший</a> (5229)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настроить.html>настро́ивший</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastróivšij</span>)

***настроить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:настроить.html>настро́ить</a> (5229)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:строить.html>стро́ить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stróitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настроить.html>настро́ить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastróitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настраивать.html>настра́ивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to build a lot</li>
<li>to tune, to tune up</li>
<li>to tune in</li>
<li>to adjust, to customize</li>
<li>to make, to dispose <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:настроить.html>настро́ить</a></b> кого́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:грустный.html>гру́стный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лада.html>лад</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nastróitʹ</b> kovó-libo na grústnyj lad</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>to make</b> someone depressed</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to incite, to incline</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настроение.html>настрое́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nastrojénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настроить.html>настро́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nastrój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***настрой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:настроить.html>настро́й</a> (13760)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настроить.html>настро́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastrój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настрой.html>настро́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настрой.html>настро́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настрой.html>настро́ев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mood, spirit</li></ol>

***наступать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наступать.html>наступа́ть</a> (2138)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ступать.html>ступа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stupátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наступать.html>наступа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastupátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наступить.html>наступи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tread, to step on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>Не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наступать.html>наступа́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пяток.html>пя́тки</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ne <b>nastupáj</b> mne na pjátki.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Do not <b>step</b> on my heels.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come, to begin, to set in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наступать.html>наступа́ют</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:холод.html>холода́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Nastupájut</b> xolodá.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The cold is <b>setting in</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:рано.html>ра́но</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:осень.html>о́сень</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наступать.html>наступа́ет</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ráno ósenʹ <b>nastupájet</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Autumn <b>is coming</b> early.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to attack, to advance, to be on the offensive
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:враг.html>Враг</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наступать.html>наступа́ет</a></b>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vrag <b>nastupájet</b>.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The enemy <b>is advancing</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***наступить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:наступить.html>наступи́ть</a> (1355)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ступить.html>ступи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наступить.html>наступи́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastupítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наступать.html>наступа́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tread, to step on
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:осторожно.html>осторо́жно</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:наступить.html>наступи́</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:котенок.html>котёнка</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ostoróžno, ne <b>nastupí</b> na kotjónka.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Be careful not to <b>step</b> on the kitten.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to come, to begin, to set in
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:наступить.html>наступи́ла</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:весна.html>весна́</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Nastupíla</b> vesná.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Spring <b>has come</b>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наступление.html>наступле́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nastuplénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>
<table style="float:right; clear:right; padding:3; margin-left:0.5em; margin-bottom:0.5em; border: 1px solid 6699CC; border-collapse:collapse;" cellpadding="2" rules="all" class="morfotable ru">
<tbody><tr>
<th bgcolor="EEF9FF"> 
</th>
<th bgcolor="EEF9FF"><a href = vnd.unilang:будущий.html>бу́дущ</a>.
</th>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наступить.html>наступи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nastupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наступление.html>наступле́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastuplénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наступление.html>наступле́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наступление.html>наступле́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:наступление.html>наступле́ний</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>offensive, onset, advance <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">an attack</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>beginning, coming</li></ol>

***настучать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:настучать.html>настуча́ть</a> (26905)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стучать.html>стуча́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stučátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настучать.html>настуча́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastučátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стучать.html>стуча́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">насту́кивать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pass information by knocking (e.g. Morse code); to knock a rhythm</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">slang</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to squeal on, to rat on</li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:настырный.html>насты́рный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nastýrnyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)насты́рнее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)насты́рней</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> pushy, aggressive, insolent, brazen</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:насущный.html>насу́щный</a> (12905)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">насѫштьнъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nasǫštĭnŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насущный.html>насу́щный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nasúščnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>vital, essential, urgent, necessary
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:хлеб.html>хлеб</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:насущный.html>насу́щный</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">xleb <b>nasúščnyj</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">bread as essential or vital necessity</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:насущный.html>насу́щный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вопрос.html>вопро́с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>nasúščnyj</b> voprós</i> ― <span class="e-translation">essential or pressing (urgent) issue</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насчитать.html>насчита́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nasčitátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насчитывать.html>насчи́тывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nasčítyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насчитать.html>насчита́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to count</li>
<li>to number</li>
<li>to include, to contain</li></ol>

***насчитываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:насчитываться.html>насчи́тываться</a> (13350)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насчитывать.html>насчи́тывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nasčítyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насчитываться.html>насчи́тываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nasčítyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">насчита́ться</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to number, to amount <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:город.html>го́роде</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:насчитываться.html>насчи́тывается</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:миллион.html>миллио́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:житель.html>жи́телей</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v étom górode <b>nasčítyvajetsja</b> millión žítelej</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the population of this city numbers [runs to, amounts to] one million</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:они.html>их</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:насчитываться.html>насчи́тываются</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тысяча.html>ты́сячи</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ix <b>nasčítyvajutsja</b> týsjači</i> ― <span class="e-translation">they number in the thousands</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насчитывать.html>насчи́тывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nasčítyvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***насыпать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:насыпать.html>насыпа́ть</a> (9785)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sýpatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насыпать.html>насы́пать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nasýpatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыпать.html>сы́пать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:насыпать.html>насыпа́ть</a></strong></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to strew, to pour <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to distribute objects or pieces of something, of friable objects, not liquids</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to sputter, to pelt, to spout</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:насыпать.html>насы́пать</a></strong></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nasýpatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насыпать.html>насыпа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nasypátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:насыпать.html>насы́пать</a></strong></b>) <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">the impf./pf. forms differ in the word stress in the infinitive and the conjugation</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>to strew, to pour <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to distribute objects or pieces of something, of friable objects, not liquids</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to sputter, to pelt, to spout</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насыпь.html>на́сыпь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">násypʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насыпь.html>на́сыпи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насыпь.html>на́сыпи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насыпь.html>на́сыпей</a></b>)

<li>dike, dam</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:насытить.html>насы́тить</a> (21648)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">на-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-сы́тить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sýtitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Not directly from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">сыти́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sytítʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to satisfy, to saturate</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> because of the differing stress pattern and iotation (<i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сыч.html>сычу́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">syčú</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> but <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насытить.html>насы́щу</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nasýšču</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насытить.html>насы́тить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nasýtitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насыщать.html>насыща́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to satisfy, to satiate, to sate</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chemistry</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to saturate</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насыщение.html>насыще́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nasyščénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насыщенный.html>насы́щенный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nasýščennyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:насыщаться.html>насыща́ться</a> (29543)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насыщать.html>насыща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nasyščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насыщаться.html>насыща́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">nasyščátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насытиться.html>насы́титься</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be full <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">after eating</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>to be saturated</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:насыщать.html>насыща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">nasyščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
